<UserId.>115622497871875532330</UserId.>< text>
After my first visit to the Cupertino store just to see their selection of bass lures (awesome by the way), I read some reviews that just did not jive with my experience, which was positive.  So I've gone back to Fisherman's Warehouse several times since in the last month or so, with each time being better than the previous.  I paid close attention to how the salespeople assisted other customers, and they were always courteous, attentive and helpful.  One example - I saw was a guy purchasing a fishing pole, but there was a discrepancy in price at the cash register.  The register said the pole was $100 less than it was marked (and it wasn't on sale- it was clearly an error), but there was no argument from the salesman and he honored the lower price, saving the customer about $100. They've definitely earned my business!< /text>

< Review>
The McDonald Avenue Target is well prepared for visitors during the pandemic. They have designated parking spots for "curbside" delivery orders. All carts and hand baskets are consistently  cleaned with disinfectants, hand sanitizer stations at the front entry points, all self-service registers and exit area. Prerecorded messages play about mandatory mask-wearing and the availability of curbside services. The store is clean and most items are readily available (meaning: not being locked up in a cabinet). I shop here frequently and really enjoy supporting this Target store.<//Review>

<Text>That is how a steak should be. Cooked to order and just to my like. The steak itself was one of the best I have had in 2018.
We stopped in for New Years Eve. Party of 2 with reservation. Quickly seated upon entry. Drinks were ordered and delivered in a prompt manor as was our salads. Drinks were amazing. Don't be afraid to dry a few and give some input on how you like your drink. Slightly sweeter or stronger tasting, they can make it to your desire without compromising alcohol quantity.
From the salads on it just kept getting better. Great salads to move the palate along. Everything moved at a nice non rushed pace allowing plenty of time for you to enjoy yourself and the company you are with.
When our main course arrived it was amazing both my steak and the salmon my gf ordered. The dry age steak was amazingly soft with a nice cut. On a side note; this is one of the best steak knifes I have ever used at a steakhouse.
The purple cauliflower dish is amazing and I highly recommend it. The mac n cheese is flavors out of this world. Serving size seems to be for (4).
All throughout this meal we got amazing service and our waitstaff was well versed in the menu.
The dessert  was a nice chocolate cake and ice cream. Very nice finish to the meal. The hot tea was an added touch. (As a tea drinker its hard to find places with quality hot tea service.) There was so many great looking desserts it was really hard to choose. More for next time I suppose.
After seeing plenty of plates move by, I think its safe to say anyone should be able to enjoy a great meal here.
Enjoy have fun and take your time! Our meal from start to finish was 2 hours and it never felt long or like we waited on anything, is was smooth and enjoyable. Prices are comparable with other steakhouses in San Diego. See you again soon!!!<//Text><pics>None</pics>< Resp>

<Response>None</Response>< Text>
Don‚Äôt waste your money here - bad steak and bad management.
I was invited by someone to eat at this restaurant, and I was very disappointed. This is the second time that I have eaten at this restaurant, and the first experience was likewise disappointing. The first experience was shortly after the restaurant opened, and I put that experience down to 'teething' issues. My host for the evening had asked me for a recommendation and I suggested that we try Larsen's again. I ordered a wet-aged NY strip steak and asked that it be prepared charred/rare. The chef cooked the steak itself perfectly, however is was totally over seasoned with salt. I am a person who likes a lot of salt on my food and I found the steak to be almost inedible. I tried to scrape off the 'crust' of the steak with my knife, but it was still extremely salty and I was only able to eat a small amount of it before giving up. Out of respect for my host, I did not want to call the manager to our table to address the issue, and I also had a hard stop at 7:30pm and there would not have been time to prepare a new steak. When ordering a steak that cost $65, at a high-end steak house where steak is the specialty of the house, I expect that the chef knows how to season the meat correctly. The seasoning was not slightly off it was completely over seasoned to the point that the steak was ruined. I eat a lot of steak and am a regular customer to both Fleming's and Truluck's in the UTC area. Donovan's, Ruths Chris and Cowboy Star are also part of my regular rotation. My first experience at this restaurant was disappointing and the second even more disappointing. I contacted the restaurant by email the next morning to tell them about my experience, and they have not bothered to respond or try and contact me in any way. I have discussed my experience with other co-workers, as our offices are in the UTC area, and they have had similar disappointing experiences, and have noticed that the restaurant is mostly empty during lunch and dinner time which would indicate that there are problems with this restaurant. I expect a lot more from a high-end  and high-priced steak restaurant, and would not spend my money here ever again. There are enough other choices out there who are doing it right and are worth the money, and I suspect that this restaurant will not survive.</Text>

On July 5, five of us visited Larsens  for a friends birthday. We typically like to enjoy a glass of wine prior to ordering. We ordered a bottle of wine, our waiter  Took the order and returned in about 10 minutes to let us know they were still waiting on the wine and what we like to go ahead and order. We said we would like to wait for the wine and we would order once it was served. Another 10 minutes went by our server came by again and said they didn't have a key to the wine cabinet that's only if the manager is allowed to have the key and he was not in attendance. He did offer us a glass of Prosecco, almost 45 minutes later I wine was finally brought to us. We asked for an apology from the manager as we found this totally unacceptable. The manager I was told when I called the next day, Cory Briggs, and asked for a callback. My call was never returned and a follow-up email to the website was not responded to.  The food was overpriced however it was quite delicious. The service was terrible and I do not believe by state law only two people are allowed to have a key to the wine which is what our waiter told us.</Review>

< Review>
I have had dinner twice just recently in the last 6 weeks and I have to say that this is an overrated and overpriced steakhouse. It's amazing that it's owned by the same company that owns Fleming's and I would not trade Fleming's for this one. The service is below standards for a steakhouse of this caliber. The first time we went the server told us the specials for the day, but never said the prices of the special items. I ordered their Waygu bone in rib-eye and when the bill came we were blown away at what they charged us ($370). Not only was the price absurd, but the steak was the worst I've ever had at any fine dinning steakhouse. We talked to the management about the fact that the server never mentioned the price of the steak, but that the steak was full of fat and not flavorful at all. Prior to my first visit my family has been to this steakhouse 4 previous times and the reason they do is because they like grass fed steaks and they offer them there. The best the manager could offer was a gift certificate for $100. Aside from the steak being outrageously priced and tasteless I asked for a glass of Prisoner wine and the server said that they were out of it and I had to let him know that the wine wall was displaying a full rack of the wine. He then came back and told me I was correct. My second visit the service was so bad that they bought us dessert. Save the time and money and go to Fleming's it's ten times better. This restaurant opened in Vegas and it did not last but 9 months. I see a short lived stint here in La Jolla too. I would not recommend this place to anyone.</Review>
